The successor to csvjson is here: an AI agent that can convert your data to and from any format, securely.

Turnkey CSV Importer • Installs in minutes

CSV or TSV JSON

To get started, upload or paste your data from Excel (saved as CSV or TSV).


Download Copy to clipboard

Need help cleaning data?

Embed all the functionality of csvjson in any web application with Flatfile. Auto-match columns, validate data fields, and provide an intuitive CSV import experience.

More Details

  • This function is available as a npm package
  • CSV stands for Comma Separated Values. Often used as an interchange data format to represent table records, one per line. CSV is plain text.
  • The CSV format is documented in an RFC memo RFC-4180.
  • The first line is often the header, or column names. Each subsequent row is a record and should have the same number of fields.
  • Fields containing the separator character, line breaks and double-quotes must be enclosed inside double quotes ".
  • Other separator are often used like tabs \tor semi-colons ;. TSV or Tab Separated Values is used to store table data in Clipboards. When data is copied from Excel for example, it is stored as TSV in the Clipboard.
  • With CSVJSON you can parse values as numbers or JSON. Turn on respective Parse Numbers and Parse JSON switches to convert valid numbers and JSON (null, false, true, [] and {}).
  • With CSVJSON you can transpose the csv before conversion. Rows become columns, and columns become rows.
  • With CSVJSON you can output a hash (or object) instead of an array. In that case, the hash key will be the first column.

View Change Log

Mar 20, 2019

Bug fix: Detect duplicate column headers and make them unique. GitHub issue #71.

Feb 2, 2019

Refactored and published npm package csv2json. Fix for GitHub issue #70.

Jan 26, 2019

Improvement: Removed 64k limit on download button. Also fixed issue #68 'Cannot work functional with special letters'.

Mar 31, 2018

Improvement: Added option to parse JSON values.

Dec 18, 2017

Improvement: Added option to minify or compact JSON. GitHub issue #21

Oct 7, 2016

Improvement: Added option to parse number values or not to retain original number formatting. GitHub issue #13

Jul 09, 2016

Fixed bug : If no text is present in a csv field, it was assigned 0 (zero) by default.

Jun 20, 2016

Bug fix: strings containing quotes and commas were prematurely cut.

Dec 30, 2015

Bug fix: drop quotes on keys of nested objects.

Nov 26, 2015

Improvement: Added options to transpose and output object instead of array.

Jan 30, 2014

Bug fix: Pasting Excel data into Textarea would cause an upload.

Jan 12, 2014

Initial release.

} } function startGame() { // בחירת הנתונים currentDataset = diff === 'easy' ? easyData : hardData; if(!currentDataset || currentDataset.length < 8) { alert("אין מספיק נתונים ב-JSON שנבחר!"); return; `; } // יצירת כפתורי קטגוריה const grid = document.getElementById('draw-categories'); grid.innerHTML = ''; categories.forEach(cat => { grid.innerHTML += ` `; }); nextDrawRound(); } function nextDrawRound() { if (currentDrawIndex >= 8) { showEndGame(); return; } const currentSettlement = sessionSettlements[currentDrawIndex]; // פאנל יישוב קודם const prevPanel = document.getElementById('draw-prev-panel'); if (drawMapSettlement) { prevPanel.classList.remove('hidden'); const mapBtn = document.getElementById('draw-map-btn'); if (drawMapSettlement['lat'] || drawMapSettlement['קו רוחב']) { mapBtn.classList.remove('hidden'); mapBtn.innerHTML = `איפה זה ${drawMapSettlement["שם יישוב"]}? 🗺️`; } else mapBtn.classList.add('hidden'); if(isDrawMapOpen) toggleDrawMap(); // סגור אם פתוח } const nameEl = document.getElementById('draw-settlement-name'); nameEl.style.opacity = 0; setTimeout(() => { nameEl.innerText = currentSettlement["שם יישוב"]; nameEl.style.opacity = 1; }, 200); } function selectDrawCategory(catId) { if (usedDrawCats.has(catId)) return; const currentSettlement = sessionSettlements[currentDrawIndex]; const catObj = categories.find(c => c.id === catId); usedDrawCats.add(catId); drawMapSettlement = currentSettlement; // חישוב הטוב ביותר לפאנל הבא let bestRank = Infinity; let bestCatLabel = ""; categories.forEach(c => { if (!usedDrawCats.has(c.id) || c.id === catId) { let r = parseInt(String(currentSettlement[c.id]).replace(/,/g, '')) || 1221; r = Math.min(r, MAX_PENALTY); if (r < bestRank) { bestRank = r; bestCatLabel = c.label; } } }); let rank = parseInt(String(currentSettlement[catId]).replace(/,/g, '')) || 1221; rank = Math.min(rank, MAX_PENALTY); totalScore += rank; // עדכון ה-UI const dot = document.getElementById(`draw-dot-${currentDrawIndex}`); dot.className = `w-3 h-3 rounded-full shadow-md scale-110 ${rank <= 150 ? 'bg-success' : rank <= 400 ? 'bg-warning' : 'bg-danger'}`; const btn = document.getElementById(`draw-cat-${catId}`); btn.disabled = true; const dataConfig = categoryDataMap[catId]; const formattedVal = dataConfig.format(currentSettlement[dataConfig.field]); btn.innerHTML = `
${catObj.icon}${catObj.label}
${currentSettlement["שם יישוב"]} ${formattedVal} מקום ${rank} `; // הכנת הודעת הפידבק שתופיע בסיבוב הבא const feedbackEl = document.getElementById('draw-prev-feedback'); if (rank === bestRank) { feedbackEl.innerHTML = `🎯 שיחוק! בחרת מושלם עבור ${currentSettlement["שם יישוב"]}.`; } else { feedbackEl.innerHTML = `עבור ${currentSettlement["שם יישוב"]}, מוטב היה לבחור ${bestCatLabel} (מקום ${bestRank})`; } gameHistory.push({ name: currentSettlement["שם יישוב"], catLabel: catObj.label, rank: rank, icon: catObj.icon, obj: currentSettlement }); document.getElementById('draw-score').innerText = totalScore.toLocaleString(); currentDrawIndex++; setTimeout(nextDrawRound, 400); // מעבר מהיר (אין צורך להמתין) } function toggleDrawMap() { const wrapper = document.getElementById('draw-map-wrapper'); const btn = document.getElementById('draw-map-btn'); isDrawMapOpen = !isDrawMapOpen; if(isDrawMapOpen) { wrapper.classList.remove('h-0', 'opacity-0', 'pointer-events-none'); wrapper.classList.add('h-40', 'opacity-100', 'mt-2'); } drawMap.invalidateSize(); const lat = drawMapSettlement['lat'] || drawMapSettlement['קו רוחב']; const lon = drawMapSettlement['lon'] || drawMapSettlement['קו אורך']; if(lat && lon) { if(drawMarker) drawMap.removeLayer(drawMarker); drawMarker = L.marker([lat, lon]).addTo(drawMap); drawMap.flyTo([lat, lon], 11, { animate: true, duration: 1.2 }); } }, 300); } else { wrapper.classList.remove('h-40', 'opacity-100', 'mt-2'); wrapper.classList.add('h-0', 'opacity-0', 'pointer-events-none'); btn.innerHTML = `איפה זה ${drawMapSettlement["שם יישוב"]}? 🗺️`; } } /* ===================================================================== מצב הצבה (Placement) ===================================================================== */ function initPlaceMode() { renderPlaceBank(); renderPlaceCategories(); } function renderPlaceBank() { const bank = document.getElementById('place-bank'); bank.innerHTML = ''; sessionSettlements.forEach((s, idx) => { // אל תציג אם הוא כבר שובץ const isPlaced = Object.values(placeAssignments).some(placed => placed["שם יישוב"] === s["שם יישוב"]); if (assigned) { grid.innerHTML += ` `; } else { grid.innerHTML += ` `; } }); } function placeInCategory(catId) { if (!selectedPlaceItem) return; placeAssignments[catId] = selectedPlaceItem; selectedPlaceItem = null; // איפוס בחירה renderPlaceBank(); renderPlaceCategories(); } function unplaceCategory(catId) { delete placeAssignments[catId]; renderPlaceBank(); renderPlaceCategories(); } function submitPlacement() { // חישוב ניקוד סופי totalScore = 0; gameHistory = []; categories.forEach(cat => { const s = placeAssignments[cat.id]; let rank = parseInt(String(s[cat.id]).replace(/,/g, '')) || 1221; rank = Math.min(rank, MAX_PENALTY); totalScore += rank; gameHistory.push({ name: s["שם יישוב"], catLabel: cat.label, rank: rank, icon: cat.icon, obj: s }); }); showEndGame(); } /* ===================================================================== מסך סיום ומפת סיכום (End Game) ===================================================================== */ function showEndGame() { document.getElementById('draw-screen').classList.add('hidden'); document.getElementById('place-screen').classList.add('hidden'); document.getElementById('modal').classList.remove('hidden'); document.getElementById('final-score').innerText = totalScore.toLocaleString(); // היסטוריה (רשימה) document.getElementById('round-history').innerHTML = gameHistory.map(h => `
${h.icon} ${h.name} (${h.catLabel}) ${h.rank}
`).join(''); // מפת סיכום! setTimeout(() => { const endMapObj = L.map('end-map', { zoomControl: false, dragging: false, scrollWheelZoom: false }); L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png').addTo(endMapObj); let bounds = []; gameHistory.forEach(h => { const lat = h.obj['lat'] || h.obj['קו רוחב']; const lon = h.obj['lon'] || h.obj['קו אורך']; if(lat && lon) { const marker = L.marker([lat, lon]).addTo(endMapObj); marker.bindPopup(`
${h.name}
${h.icon} ${h.catLabel}
מקום ${h.rank}
`); bounds.push([lat, lon]); } }); if(bounds.length > 0) { endMapObj.fitBounds(bounds, { padding: [20, 20] }); } else { endMapObj.setView([31.5, 34.8], 7); // ברירת מחדל ישראל אם אין קואורדינטות } }, 300); confetti({ particleCount: 200, spread: 90, origin: { y: 0.6 } }); } function shareResults() { const emojis = gameHistory.map(h => h.rank < 150 ? '🟩' : h.rank < 400 ? '🟨' : '🟥').join(''); const text = `משחק היישובים V2 📍\n` + `מצב: ${diff === 'easy' ? 'קל' : 'קשה'} | ${mode === 'draw' ? 'הגרלה' : 'הצבה'}\n` + `תוצאה: ${totalScore} נק'\n` + `${emojis}\n` + `${window.location.href}`; if (navigator.share) { navigator.share({ text }); } else { navigator.clipboard.writeText(text); alert("הועתק ללוח!"); } }
